Dreams of High and Sacred Nature

We humans are thinking about something. We are also trying to do something. We are searching for something. So what is that something? When we put it all together, we can express it as a dream. 
Everyone has dreams and strives to achieve them. 

This applies equally to men and women, to families and nations, and it leads to a continuous conclusion that if there is a world, it is the same for the world. When we expand our view of the world, we see that there is a visible world and an invisible world, and both the visible and invisible worlds have dreams. If there is some absolute God who created this entire universe, that absolute God must also think, desire, and want to do something, so it is certain that He also has dreams. 
However, if those dreams are chaotic and we think we are standing in the midst of that chaos, how much turmoil will there be in families, societies, nations, and the world? It would be chaotic. 
If we turn in a certain way, it can be fun and pleasant, but if we turn this way and that way chaotically, it becomes confusing. When there is a counterpart and we say, "Ah, I am turning," that is when we find our center. What do we mean by turning? When there is a counterpart, it turns well, and when we let go, it is okay too. Even if I roll like this, if I say, "I roll to eliminate that protruding thing over there," then that is also acceptable. 
When you look at something without focus, what do you call that? What happens when you move your eyes without any standard? However, when you focus, it is not confusion but normal. 
It is easy to think that dreams are like that. Dreams seem to lack order and purpose, just something that happens. When we think of dreams, it seems vague. 
When we talk about dreams, there must be a high purpose and direction, and we can conclude that. So what kind of dream do we want to have? We want to have a noble dream. 
The destination of the dream of beauty is love. 
If there were a machine that could fulfill dreams, what would be the best dream? What would be the heaviest dream? Would it be an expensive dream? (Laughter) For women, it would be beauty. For men, it would be being strong and masculine. (Laughter) 
No matter how beautiful a woman is, if that beauty has no purpose, what would happen? Would you like a beautiful doll in a box? If you say, "You, being such a beauty, just sit there all day," women would all run away. (Laughter) Is sitting there the ideal type of beauty? Is it to be out and about? To become beautiful, a woman must go to where women are, to seek out beauty. Isn’t that right? 
Since all women are beautiful, how wonderful is that! (Laughter) So what is the dream of beauty? If beauty itself has a dream, what is that dream? If beauty has a dream, what is that dream? 
Is it to find a more beautiful woman? "No." Then what is it? If there is a most beautiful queen, do we go to find that queen, and then where do we go next? "Ah, success!" That is not it. We must go further. No matter how beautiful the queen is, even if she becomes a queen, we cannot stop there; we must go further. If we say it is good, will beauty dance there? Where do we go? 
If beauty has a dream, what would that dream be? "Make someone happy." Make someone happy. That is the truth. Then what is someone? "Man." Man. A woman goes to the man. If the dream of beauty stops at the man, does that feel good? "Yes." Why is that? Why is it "yes"? We must understand that the dream itself is not just the man; there is something else among the men. What could that be? "God's love." Whether it is God's love or true love, love is the same. (Laughter) The dream of beauty, once established, can find its destination in love. That conclusion has been reached. 
An ideal dream must be realized through ideal harmony. 
The same goes for men. What is the purpose of being strong and all that? Is it to be a champion of physical beauty, to boast of being a world champion in the ring? 
For example, if you become a boxing champion and the audience is cheering, would you prefer a big, strong man to come and give you a bouquet, or a pretty woman to come and give it to you? Would you prefer a big person giving you a world-sized bouquet, or a beautiful person bringing you a small flower with a smile? Which would you prefer? "A beautiful person giving it." Why is that? Why? That is harmony. It is because we need the beauty of harmony. How wonderful would it be if a strong and scary man harmonized with a small and non-threatening woman? 
When I see Westerners, their eyes are blue, their features are sharp, but their noses are all narrow and high. Imagine if you attached an Eastern woman's nose to a Western woman's face. How mismatched would that be? Also, Eastern people have flat and round faces. If their faces are round and their eyes are long, but their noses are narrow and high, how ugly would that be? How ridiculous! But because the nose is flat, it harmonizes. (Laughter) 
When looking at the world-famous Mona Lisa, a sad person feels sad, while a happy person feels happy. Each person's thoughts differ according to their feelings. Because it resonates differently in everyone's heart, it is considered a masterpiece. It is harmony; it is harmonized. Do you understand what I mean? Everything is like that. Do you think so? "Yes." What is the ideal dream? Now you understand. We can deduce that the ideal dream can be realized in ideal harmony. 
We humans have many dreams. Don’t you all have dreams? Do you have dreams? "Yes." And men too? "We have them." Are those dreams for oneself, to harmonize oneself, or are they dreams to harmonize with the whole? "Dreams to harmonize with the whole." Is that so? What kind of woman has an ideal dream? "A beautiful woman, but not someone who boasts of her beauty. Isn’t the dream of a beautiful woman to harmonize the beauty of the whole? Isn’t that the ideal? Therefore, no matter how beautiful she is, she should not smile for herself. Everything she sees, says, thinks, and does should be like that. Then all the worlds related to that beautiful woman will harmonize. That is not the Mona Lisa in a frame at the Louvre, but our living Mona Lisa. 
If such a woman exists, what will men do? All men's dreams will flock to her. Isn’t that right? What will they do? A man would say, "Hey, this is my beauty." Then the woman would kick him out. Why does she kick him out? Because a man who destroys the harmony of the whole must be expelled. A man who destroys the beauty of the whole must be expelled. That is good. That is truth. That is reality. 
To be the counterpart of such a woman, a man must possess a personality that can harmonize with the whole. Then naturally, they will become one. Everything is like that. So if those two harmonize and move, we can think that the universe harmonizes. What is at the center? It is centered around higher love. If that is the case, will all the people in the human world, that is, men and women, open their mouths and look? Will they not? What will they do? 
If that is the case, what about the world, the heavens and the earth? It is the same. Do you think it will be distorted or not? "That’s right." Also, if God exists, what will God do? "Hey, you guys! That’s not right. You need to break that ugly thing!" Will He say that? "No." God would be the same. If God has eyes, His eyes would be focused like that, and His ears would be focused like that, and all senses and emotions would be focused like that. 
Then, when we draw this whole conclusion, if there is such a love that is ideally harmonized, if we just pull that, the universe can harmonize eternally, day and night, throughout history, across past, present, and future, with only true love existing, that is the conclusion. 
If I turn like this, how wonderful would it be to be wrapped in that thread of love? When we say we are wrapped in the thread of love, does it feel bad? We would want to be wrapped forever. We would be happy to move forever. Also, if we are pulled from the other side, we would want to be released forever. There we can find the concept of eternal give-and-take. Today, in the Unification Church, we talk about give-and-take. Where does eternal give-and-take start? Eternal give-and-take is only possible from such love.

"Right."

**Center and My Position**

When you think of the concept of 'I', where is the center of my being? Some people say the eyes are the center, while others say the hands are the center. Those who are skilled with their hands say the hands are the center, and those who are intelligent say the head is the center. It varies depending on how one thinks.

Moreover, in our Unification Church, we understand that a person is composed of a dual structure. There is a physical body and at the same time, a spiritual body.

The most important thing for a person is love. 

So, can these two exist separately? What should be done? If the body claims to be the center, it cannot lead the mind wherever it wants, and if the mind claims to be the center, it cannot lead the body wherever it wants. If these two beings do not unite, it is a contradiction.

So, when do they become one? Have you thought about it? This is the mind, and this is the body. (He writes while speaking) For them to become one, there must be a center. A center that both the body and the mind like is necessary.

Our Pride

What is pride? What is the definition of pride? It is something you want to reveal. It is something you want to reveal. If you look around here, there are white people, black people, and yellow people, various races gathered together. Now, let us think about each other boasting. Think about it.

Definition of Pride
Now, let’s think about white people boasting among themselves. That would be different from a white person boasting to a black or Asian person. The content, taste, and preference would all be different than when white people boast among themselves. Also, black people have their own pride. Yellow people have their own pride as well.
